\[8z - \frac{8z}{m} = 10\left(\frac{8z}{m}\right)\left(50 - \frac{8z}{m}\right).\]
Simplifying this equation gives us
\[m^2 - 10m + 40 = 0.\]

\[8z + z = 50.\]
Solving this equation gives us $z = 5$.
